id="popover-content-70de7f89-742f-4f41-8cd8-c28e874c208b"><h3 class="wt-text-caption-title wt-mb-xs-1">Tips for a great title:</h3><ul class="wt-mb-xs-2"><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Clearly state the item for sale, like "mug" or "dress"</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Include the most important traits upfront, like your item's color, material, and size</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Streamline for clarity and scannability. Consider using less than 15 words when including the traits that make your item special.</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Only include holidays, special occasions, or recipient types if they're essential to what the item is, like "birthday candle" or "Halloween costume"</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Move subjective words, like "perfect" or "beautiful," to the description</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Try not to repeat words</li><li class="wt-text-caption">Don't worry about adding info about price, shipping, or sales. Etsy helps take care of this by badging your items in Search.</li></ul><p class="wt-mb-xs-2 wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption"><a data-clg-id="WtTextLink" target="_blank" href="https://www.etsy.com/seller-handbook/article/1399426136697" class="wt-sem-text-primary wt-text-link">Learn more about suggested titles<span class="wt-screen-reader-only">Opens a new tab</span></a></p><span class="wt-popover__arrow"></span></div></div></label><p id="listing-title-helper-text" class="wt-text-caption wt-display-block  wt-mb-xs-1">A good title focuses on your item
